- **OCC** indicates an ethoxy group (ethyl group attached to oxygen).
- Thus, the molecule is **hexyl ethanoate** (or ethyl hexanoate), an ester with the formula CH₃(CH₂)₅C(=O)OCH₂CH₃.

Esters typically have moderate polarity due to the carbonyl and ether-like oxygen atoms, and their properties often depend on the length of the carbon chains and the presence of other functional groups.

- Methyl nonanoate (~10 carbons total) has a value of -2.64.
- The target molecule has 8 carbons total, closer to methyl nonanoate but not as extreme.

- Difference in carbons between isopropyl acetate and methyl nonanoate: 10 - 4 = 6 carbons.
- Difference in property value: 0.17 - (-2.64) = 2.81.
- Per carbon change: 2.81 / 6 ≈ 0.47 decrease per carbon.
- From isopropyl acetate (4 carbons) to target (8 carbons): 8 - 4 = 4 carbons.
- Expected decrease: 4 * 0.47 ≈ 1.88.

Additionally, the ethyl group in the target molecule (vs. methyl in methyl nonanoate) might slightly increase polarity, making the value less negative.
